<user_name>mj Deejay<//user_name>< review>
This business is not considerate of Covid-19 protocol:

At least two employees here (manager + chef?) do not wear masks. I have been here multiple times and seen this. They were talking closely with customers, handling money, and takeout.

When confronted and asked why they are not wearing masks, they responded that they have a respiratory / medical issue allowing them mask exempt status.

This has been thoroughly debunked by doctors- the idea that masks obstruct oxygen intake. The fact that this restaurant has employees working without masks during a pandemic is disrespectful to the many people sacrificing to reduce spread of contagion.

Avoid this restaurant at all costs if you care about masks being worn by the employees.

I would like to see the business owner's response to this situation. Are you supporting your employees not wearing masks?

Regarding Food and Service: It took 45min for a "ready in 15min" order. Considering the food experience has been average, this place is not worth the risk to your health for the benefit of the nutrition.< /review>

< Review>
I am sorry to give this place a bad review. It's nothing personal, I wish them success I just really didn't enjoy my experience here.

Service:
We were asked 5+ times if we were ready to order. Our server would circle around and ask after a couple minutes or so. We had a hard time deciding on what to order and felt very rushed. Not only did our server ask us multiple times but we even had another server from a different section ask us. It felt very pushy and awkward. Once we finally did order it took forever for our meal to arrive, we waited for a long time for the Verde Enchiladas.

Food:
The food looked presentable but didn't have much flavor.

Verde Enchiladas had very bland filling, sweet potato hash was lacking flavor. The rice was over cooked and mushy. The beans were soupy and again bland.

Raw Roll was ok, wasn't terrible but there was something that tasted very bitter. Flavor combination wasn't very appealing or tasty.

Sad to say I will not be returning to this restaurant.< /Review>

<text>Got off the plane one day, typed in Vegan restaurants on Happy Cow and came up with THE BEST cooked/plant based vegan restaurant in San Diego. I've been back now 6x in the last few months and highly suggest giving this place a try!!  The horchata was a great start followed by the cauliflower ceviche and the guacamole (we were starving) Yum! The experience there with both owner and staff had me very excited about coming back to town to try more of her menu. Thank God that I did. The next time I came to town I went back to the village determined to give her sushi a try. What an experience!! The owner is a very beautiful soul, bound and determined to boost immune systems through the love and effort she puts into her food. Very wise and educated on health issues and safety, she's gone further than most to educate herself on the current state of affairs and is very knowledgable on what true health and wellness looks like in a time of severe misinformation on what humans need to be doing to avoid any sort of virus or sickness. Super impressed, her staff is very nice, very educated people and its far and away the best plant based sushi I've EVER had!! <name>Seng Saeliew</name>< time>
1534766536667<//time>
<Rating>5</Rating><review>This location is one of my favorite for late night grub spot. There are a few that are along International Blvd. I will go through some of them quickly and what type of scene the spot contains n their specialty.

1. Tacos Mi Rancho
Location: International Blvd n 1st Ave
Scene: Popular with the transient Americans as it doesn't have any of the raunchy scene you would normally encounter with the others. Specialty: Carnitas n Veggie Burrito

2. Taqueria Sinaloa
Locational: International Blvd n 22nd Ave
Scene: Popular w/both the locals n new transient that dwells within the vicinity. Has decent parking, tables n a second truck within feet of each other. Glimpse of working women can be scene in plain sight during the day but more prevalent at night.
Specialty: Shrimp Tacos n overall burrito

3. Mi Grullense Taco Truck
Location: International Blvd n 30th Ave
Scene: Popular with the local Mexicans, Paisa n other Latin group. Good size parking space available compare to the previous scene. Similar raunchy scene of working women can be seen from this location as well. Best to keep to yourself and stay within sight of the Taco truck for your own safety.
Specialty: They are good for their overall menu but on the drier end of the spectrum where it's okay with locals but not for my pallette.

4. Tacos El Gordo
Location: International Blvd n 42nd Ave
Scene: Popular w/lots of locals n heavy traffic scene. Expect long wait especially during the late night when things heat up. Parking can be hectic so plan ahead n bring some drinks while your at it. Party in the back parking lot away from the prying eyes of the police and enjoy your food.
Specialty: Overall good food but the portions tends to be smaller than the other stalls. They make up for it by offering moist n delicious tacos. A lot more pricier than I would have like. The owners have been inflating the price for the last 3-4 years. The reason is for this is to fund their other new location while retaining their profit quotas.

5. El Taco Zamorano
Location: International Blvd n High St. Their other location is a few blocks down on 48th Ave.
Scene: Pretty much a dead scene for the most part.
Specialty: There isn't anything that really stands out on this scene. This is the definition of meh quality where it just is a waste of your time. Parking is limited and this also deters a bit of traffic from coming through.

6. Tacos Guadalajara
Location: International Blvd n 44th Ave
Scene: Hidden gem with the locals w/enough parking. The outside place has been remodeled w/seating n good lighting. The views however is dead as the location is on the farther end of the International Blvd where not too many venture to. It's also only fees away from a halfway house so beggers are a common scene here. Other than the usual asking for hand out...they usually do not bother the patrons.
Specialty: This place is considered the second best options to going to El Gordo and I really do wish that they will catch on in time in offering home grilled serrano peppers versus can jalape√±os from the store. It really makes a big difference...the cost is little but the difference is huge. Hopefully they are reading this.

Tacos Guadalajara is my favorite scene as it tends to be quite and I can enjoy my meal out of of trunks while just minding my own business. If I'm with my friends n the night is still young then no doubt I will be over at El Gordo w/a bottle of Hennessey and 20 tacos for the friends n I.< /review>< Pics>

<pictures>None</pictures>< Review>
This place is a very solid, no frills Indian restaurant. We went with three other people after attending a movie at the Indian Film Festival down the street a few weeks ago (~2pm). The place wasn't crowded, as they were an hour away from closing for a few hours before their dinner shift. Service was very friendly and relatively quick. They have an extensive vegetarian section of the menu, as well as meat and fish, so there's really something for everyone! You can choose to get your dishes mild, medium or spicy. They're known for their spicy, but we got everything medium, out of concern spicy may be too much and not fun to eat. Medium wasn't bad at all, but I could see how spicy may be too much! (Side note, my stomach didn't feel great afterward, which I attribute to the spice more than the food).</Review>

<rate>5< /rate>< text>
We live in LA, so we usually do take-out. However, we've eaten at the restaurant and had the same wonderful experience. As others have pointed out, this restaurant is in a strip mall, so it isn't really anything to write home about. Nevertheless, the food is outstanding! I LOVE the chicken Bhuna, Vindaloo, and Butter dishes. If you like it spicy, they will deliver! One great part of dinning in is BYOB policy with NO extra charge. If you forget, there is a convenience store in the same strip. So, if you are doing LA on a budget but still want to enjoy an evening meal, give Crown of India the chance to impress you with their food!</text>

<userid>117468088477759452017<//userid>< Name>
Annie Bennette<//Name>
<Time>1598599264403</Time><rate>4< /rate>< Text>
What a wonderful experience, an absolute must! I had a reservation for 4. When you arrive, you check in with your ID, then are greeted by the hostesses and taken to your table. The indoor vibe was dope as we walked through the restaurant to the outdoor seating area (make sure to bring a jacket if you are coming in the evening as I didn't see any space heaters). Also, don't plan to stay at your table all day, even though you're going to never want to leave- reservation windows are only for 90 minutes. There are no TVs.

We were then greeted by our flower hostess who took our order from the perfectly curated Cannabis menu followed by our food server who had recommendations about the food. For only being open for a few days, I was impressed with the knowledge of the staff. One suggestion would be to have something to roll up your weed on the table. I was excited to see that the matches, crutch pack, papers, and hemp papers were all complimentary.

We ordered the nachos, mac and cheese bites, corn dogs, burger, grilled cheese, pork sandwich and chocolate sunday. Absolute must haves include the ice cream sunday and the vegan nachos. I'm not a vegan and don't usually like vegan food but these were exceptional. Now onto the ice cream sunday...it was an experience. From the caramelized banana to the toasted marshmallow to the amazing brownie. I would come back and just order the sunday with an order of fries.<//Text>

I went to Akbars with a few friends, I was delighted with the very modern decor, it obviously has had some money thrown at it! The atmosphere was buzzing as it was a Saturday night, and it was the perfect start for a night out on the town. < UserId.>
107626093985872632622<//UserId.>
<Pics>None</Pics><Rating>5<//Rating><gmap_id>0x80c2bf211d3eff55:0x38d8c5872ff10080</gmap_id>< review>
Best Indian food in Los Angeles!  I admit that I have a healthy addiction to Indian food.  I've been to nearly every Indian restaurant in Los Angeles and many in other countries as well.

The lunch specials are a great deal, and are served every day except Sunday from 11am to 3pm.  Dinner portions are large, and it's great to share some entrees with others, small party or table of ten!

My favorires:

Chicken Tikka Masala - tender, marinated chicken smothered in a mouth watering, somewhat smokey flavored Masala sauce.  I like it spicy!

Saag - creamed spinach, always freshly prepared and never watery, spiced to order.

Veggie Korma - Coconut flavored curry, really amazing!

Chana Masala - Garbanzo beans simmered in Masala sauce, spiced with some fire if you like!

I could go on for pages, but this would be a very long review.  About as authentic as it gets without traveling to India, I'd say. Nice ambience, great service and feels more like visiting a family for dinner than going to a restaurant.  Alright, all this talk has me hungry, so I must head over there again soon!< /review>

<time>1565104821219< /time><rating>5< /rating><Text>The best Indian that I have found in LA!

Great flavor and spice and always pefectly cooked.

Favorite Entrees:
Chicken Vindaloo (curry, potato, tomato, lemon)
Regular Curry or the Jalfrazzi (curry w/ bell pepper, onion, garlic)
Mahkni (Buttery Sauce) try with fish or lamb.

When I order for a group I prefer to get the flavorful Pulao Rice (basmati rice, green peas & onion) and extra garlic Naan w/ basil.

Great place to order vegetarian! Their tofu passes the test but I really enjoyed the Began Bharta (roasted eggplant).

Bookmark this place!

p.s. not the Paneer but the cheese naan (cheddar Jack filled) is delicious almost like a quesadilla and great add-on for picky kids!<//Text><pictures>None</pictures><Resp>{'time': 1565123058111, 'text': 'Hey Joseph. <Text>I‚Äôm very surprised by all the 5 star reviews.  I do agree that the office staff and some, not all, nurses are warm, friendly, and courteous, as well as there being a short wait time, however I do not believe the doctors (at least the one I saw) are knowledgeable, courteous, caring, and helpful.  My experience was quite the opposite.

Firstly, I was assigned to Dr. Arlet Sarkissian as my primary physician, a very green doctor, by my new HMO.  When I explained everything that I needed during my visit, she became agitated and had a mini meltdown saying I needed to come back for more visits (basically saying she can‚Äôt help me during that visit).  Not helpful at all, and clearly not someone who I can respect or trust with my health (emotional immaturity speaks volumes).

Additionally, being someone with a chronic condition having seen many doctors over my lifetime, I knew by the questions she was asking me that she clearly had no idea what she was doing.  An example of this was when I showed her my insulin pens so she knew which insulin to prescribe me, she asked me why all the pens were set to zero.  I explained that the pens were set to zero because I was currently not dosing (you only set the pens to the amount of insulin you choose to inject at the time of injection - which a doctor should know).

Long story short, I have no confidence in the capabilities of the doctors at this facility due to my experience with Dr. Arlet Sarkissian.  Although it may not be fair to throw all the doctors at this facility in the same category, I have no desire to take chances with any other doctor there. The service was okay..I was greeted a few times by the same barista who was preparing a drink which was nice and kind of odd..( I wasn't sure whether he was going to help me with my order or not)..I was finally helped by another nice worker.. although after taking my order, he didn't take my name ..or thank me or tell me the transactin qas finished which I am not used to.  This place is busy in the morning for a weekday which is fair but it is also packed ..maybe that's why the customer service was a bit off. My drink was made in a timely manner, considering there were a lot of people waiting. The biggest distraction I noticed was how dirty it was for a Starbucks establishment. I didn't want to start snapping away with my phone, but the windows were streaked. I saw water streaks on the clear glass on the counter. The floor had garbage, the mirrors had finger tracings/drawings on them and overall, it was just the dirtiest starbucks I have ever been to. The one I normally go to is Evergreen which has less workers.. just at busy at times but I always see them cleaning and making sure everything was in order.</Review>
